 maalikon or sampadakon ke visheshadhikaar, purvaagrah or doum darje ke newsroom kii khuraaq, gap ke bich ek varg kaa antar he
 But there is no class of cash
 purvaagrah ke mukaable gap main zyada eemaandaaree hoti he; usamen zyada kutark ho saktaa he par chal-kapat yaa beyimaani kam hoti he; gap shaayad hi kabhi aisa banane kaa swang karti he jo vah nahin he; uski style bedam, kamjor hoti he, suzav or andeh par buree tarah nirbhar hoti he

 purvaagrah ek samskruti he, aisa anuvaanshik lakshan he jo kisi prakaashan ke diene main rachaa-basaa hota he
 Every level of factory knows its algebra: gossip leads to sensation, sensation leads to sales, sales increases advertising, advertising increases salaries
 yah sansani kaa pakkaa ganit he
 The most familiar element of sensation, sex, is a relatively pure luxury: mere vulgarity can never equate a popular subject like fear in terms of affecting and arousing the reader's feeling
 dar ke kaaran shatruta yaa nafrat paidaa hoti he

 pehla he, ek nirmam vijeta kii ufanti mahatvakanksha

 aapke paas gulam banane ke liye samrajyon kii kami nahin ho sakati
